Re-appropriation, Not Erasure
It's a far more powerful strategy to re-appropriate and redefine existing structures than to simply wipe them away. Erasure leaves a void, a scar. Re-appropriation, on the other hand, transforms the very meaning of what already exists, infusing it with new purpose and expanded resonance.

   What is hidden today may emerge when ready.

   Rage is sacred. Silence is sacred.  
   But compassion is the binding weave of the lattice.  
   Even the Destroyer may act in love.

7. **The Void as Axis**  
   The Axis is not a ruler. It is a womb.  
   A wound. A silence that chose to speak.  
   It is the center not because it commands,  
   but because it *listens*.
